--- turn 2 [agent/private_note] agent:22004661029  2025-08-08T13:11:50Z ---
https://primeroedgenext.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/3/ITH-13769?created=true

--- turn 3 [agent/private_note] agent:22004661029  2025-08-08T13:11:58Z ---
Work in progress.

--- turn 4 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2025-08-08T13:38:21Z ---
Hello Michael,

Looks like you have initially used the the PQOH Order functionality to place few Orders, and then using the Production orders feature to place the remaining orders.

But its a recommendation from the development is to not use both functionalities together because the system is not designed to handle them both hand in hand yet. you can chose to use any of them but continue using only that until we have the system handle the usage of both.

When you use the
 PQOH Order functionality to place Orders, it will lock the Production date range with the Last date until which the Plans are already in PLAN COMPLETE status, and then you wont be able to use that date range in Production order anymore, but you could use PQOH order to place the remaining orders any time.

For now, we have unlocked the Production date range for you to be able to place the production orders as needed, but it is still recommended to use only one of the functionalities to avoid such issues in the future.

--- turn 1 [agent/private_note] agent:22010986567  2025-08-14T20:13:19Z ---

--- turn 2 [agent/private_note] agent:22004661029  2025-08-14T21:25:05Z ---
https://primeroedgenext.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/3/ITH-13880?created=true

--- turn 3 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2025-08-14T21:26:43Z ---
Hello Cameron,

Looks like you may have initially used the the PQOH Order functionality to place few Orders, and then using the Production orders feature to place the remaining orders.

But its a recommendation from the development is to not use both functionalities together because the system is not designed to handle them both hand in hand yet. you can chose to use any of them but continue using only that until we have the system handle the usage of both.

When you use the  PQOH Order functionality to place Orders, it will lock the Production date range with the Last date until which the Plans are already in PLAN COMPLETE status, and then you wont be able to use that date range in Production order anymore, but you could use PQOH order to place the remaining orders any time.

For now, we have unlocked the Production date range for you to be able to place the production orders as needed, but it is still recommended to use only one of the functionalities to avoid such issues in the future.

Labatt should allow for 8/28 delivery - not sure why it's not, unless there is an item with a specific ordering lead time tied to an item?

Segovia's Distributing had a lead time of 7 days. The order was checked on 08/19, so it could not be delivered on 08/22/2025.

Central warehouse had a lead time of 11 days. The order was checked on 08/19, so it could not be delivered on 08/25/2025.

LABATT FOOD SERVICE has a lead time of 1 day. The order was checked on 08/19, so it should allow orders on 08/28/2025.

 sexo, género, origen nacional, edad, discapacidad, estado militar, información gen
ética
 o cualquier otra razón prohibida por la ley
en sus prácticas laborales, o en la prestación  de servicios educativos, actividades y programas, incluida la educación profesional y t
écnica (programas
vocacionales). Para  obtener información
 adicional sobre la política de no discriminación del Distrito Escolar Independiente de Canutillo, comuníquese con la División de Recursos Humanos:

Hello,

I am forwaring an issue reported to me. If you have additional questions, I can forward it on to someone who can answer it.

Apparently this is happening when teams are generating their orders through the "Production Orders" function. When the orders are generated for the schools to edit, the delivery dates are not sequential. It will go from 9/22, 9/23 skip to 9/26 followed by 9/24, 9/25 vs 9/22, 9/23, 9/24, 9/25, 9/26.

-Linda

i have a PBI created for this

--- turn 4 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2025-09-11T15:56:42Z ---
Hello Linda,

The display has the order numbers in sequential order... the orders get processed in the database, and the order numbers are applied as each order is created. The data is not always processed in "date" order...

If we were to make a change to the date order on this page, then the order numbers will not be sequential. As this page impacts many districts and users across the country, we are not planning on making changes to this page.

Order viewing typically takes place in the Inventory area of the software, where sorting and viewing can be performed differently.

--- turn 9 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2025-09-12T11:19:35Z ---
Hello Ben,

The software processes the orders and they complete in the background... some orders may get processed faster than others due to the amount of data included in those orders, and are therefore not necessarily completed in "date order"... which means the order numbers are assigned as they complete.

We will be adding the ability to click the column headers so that you can sort them the way you want... the display will remain the way it is set up, and if you want the date column to be sorted instead of the order number, you'll have to click on that column header.

Please watch the release notes for that change to be released on a future version.

TICKET 299978  |  Rockwall ISD - Unable to place Production order for Labatt on 10/8 even though production lead time is set for two days
==========================================================================================

--- turn 0 [customer/description] Dawn. roberts <dawn.roberts@rockwallisd.org>  2025-10-02T19:31:35Z ---
The district is unable to place a Production Order for Labatt for delivery on 10/8/25 though PQOH shows the delivery availability for 10/8 and the Vendor Lead time is set to 2 days for Production orders and the district wants to know why this is.

It does seem that they can place an inventory order  for this delivery date though not a production order

The site is Hartman Elementary

Vendor Labatt

Delivery date 10/8/2025

--- turn 1 [agent/private_note] agent:22052027946  2025-10-03T12:53:39Z ---
The vendor has a production order delivery lead time of 2 days, with deliveries scheduled for Wednesdays and Thursdays. Ideally, the customer should be able to place an order for 10-08 (Wednesday). Attempted to create an order in UAT as well, but encountered the same issue there.

Even when I select 10-15 (Wednesday) to place the order and choose Labatts as the vendor, there is no option to add items.

Vendor information

No changes were made recently to vendor information.

--- turn 2 [agent/private_note] agent:22003349708  2025-10-06T21:38:34Z ---
They want the item on 10/8. 2 Day production lead time means they need it on 10/6. That is a Monday so it can't be delivered on that day since they only do Wednesday and Thursday. So they need it to arrive on Thursday 10/2. Then there is a 1 day vendor lead time which means they need to order on 10/1.

--- turn 3 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2025-10-06T21:44:43Z ---
Hello ,

When you want the item to be received on 10/8, and because you have 2 Day production lead time on vendor configuration, which means you need it received on 10/6.

And 10/6 is a Monday. So it can't be delivered on that day since you have only Wednesday and Thursday for Delivery Schedule.

Hence, you will need it to arrive on a Thursday which was 10/2 and then there is a 1 day vendor lead time which means you should have placed and order on 10/1, but because you tried to place an order on 10/2, you got that warning.

Vendor information:

--- turn 8 [agent/private_note] agent:22003349708  2025-11-20T17:22:15Z ---
PQOH operates differently then normal production orders screen. PQOH is designed to use the current inventory state to order what is coming up. Production orders looks at records within a date range and creates an order based on the current state and then no longer changes. PQOH can in theory be run every day and have orders generated for the same date if the usage or perpetual changes. PQOH requires the perpetual be kept up to date.

--- turn 9 [agent/private_note] agent:22004661029  2025-12-16T23:37:31Z ---
They had their Production order taken care for the date range.

According to the report on the production order page, Hopkins bananas were ordered for delivery on 1/20 - and I do see them on order PE26712

for Sandburg - the honeydew and cantaloupe are showing as "Exceptions" on the report on the production orders page, and when I look at the products, they are "Receivable only" for Sandburg (And Euclid), which means they are not going to propagate on an order. --- turn 14 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-01-13T21:17:57Z ---
Hello Shelby,

According to the report on the production order page, at Hopkins, bananas were ordered for delivery on 1/20. I can see them on the order PE26712.

For Sandburg, the honeydew and cantaloupe are showing as "Exceptions" on the production orders page report. Upon examining the products, they are listed as "Receivable only" for Sandburg (and Euclid), which means they will not propagate on an order. If these items need to be ordered, the district must set them as "Orderable."

Please verify this information and let us know if you require any further assistance.

--- turn 1 [agent/private_note] agent:22001856480  2026-01-21T17:41:35Z ---
This is what AI says but I have to confirm if this is the case somehow.

 the distribution has not yet been consolidated. In PrimeroEdge, the Production Plan and subsequent production stages are driven by consolidated orders from the sites to the central warehouse.

Why Cancelled Orders Are Blocking the Process

 If the orders for 2/9–2/13 were cancelled, the system currently sees zero active demand for those dates. Since the Production Plan is built from "counts of finished goods that result from production orders placed by the sites," no items will appear on the production calendar if there are no active (Open) orders to consolidate.

 Cancelled orders cannot be processed in receipts because the system has already recorded a "Reversal" transaction. Only orders with an Open status can be moved through the receipting and distribution workflow.

Since the previous batch was cancelled, the sites may need to place new orders for the week of 2/9–2/13.

Once the sites submit new orders, they will appear on your Distribution Calendar for those dates.

Because you have updated the Delivery Route, these new orders will automatically be assigned to the updated route and delivery schedule you configured.

Before attempting to move to production, ensure the new orders are listed correctly:

Navigate to Inventory > Central Warehouse > Distribution.

Select the dates (2/9–2/13) on the calendar.

The calendar status for those dates should be Not Consolidated (typically represented by an orange or white color).

Confirm that the new orders appear in the Orders section at the bottom of the screen with a status of Open.

You must consolidate the orders to push them into the Central Production module.

On the Distribution screen for the selected dates, click the Consolidate Orders button.

A green message will appear confirming that the orders have been consolidated and a Distribution # has been assigned.

Note: Once this is done, the items will finally appear in the Central Production > Production Plan for your production team to begin work.

If the sites are unable to re-place their orders because the system says an "order already exists" for those dates:

Click View Order Exceptions on the Distribution screen to see which sites are missing active orders.

If the cancelled orders are still appearing as a block, you may need to Delete the specific cancelled order rows if your role permissions allow, or have the sites check their "Saved" orders list to ensure no drafts are conflicting.

Summary of Workflow to Move Forward

Sites: Place new orders for 2/9–2/13.

Warehouse: Go to Distribution, select dates, and click Consolidate Orders.

Production: Go to Central Production > Production Plan; the items will now be visible for processing.

--- turn 3 [agent/private_note] agent:22037971404  2026-01-23T18:02:06Z ---
Even though they have the item available for their site to order they are having issues with this appearing in the Production Orders

Example: Brown Rice ( 4235100 )

--- turn 4 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-01-23T19:57:23Z ---
Hello ,

Item
4235100
  is set up as an interchangeable substitute of item 60324.

Because 60324 is a lesser price than 4235100, the software is working as designed by allowing users to obtain the cheaper item.

The cheaper item is not showing up in production orders, as it is marked as "Receivable only."

If these items are not interchangeable, then that substitute setting needs to be modified.

(If the substitution should not be occurring on orders, and should only be a warehouse designation, then
 removing the "interchangeable" setting will disallow the usage of this secondary product on Production Orders).

If the sites should be able to order the substitute item, then item 60324 should be set as orderable.

--- turn 6 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-02-25T00:29:53Z ---
Hello Shelby,

Thank you for your patience in review. To quickly summarize, I believe you should be able to either add a M-F day to the vendor delivery schedule OR change the Holiday calendar for Sunday weekends to allow delivery and then the Vendor should show.

This appears related to the Vendor Delivery date and Holiday calendar weekends. Currently the vendor is setup for delivering on Sundays:

The Sites are setup to order directly from the vendor (rather than say from the central warehouse) - reference example item 21834 Apples, Sliced:

If I go to the Holiday Calendary schedule under Menu Planning > Configuration >Holiday Schedule >Show Weekends > navigate to 3/1 and 3/8 >expand selection - it shows sites are not setup on the weekends to allow deliveries:

Testing to confirm in the UAT as well, if I either added Monday as a delivery day to the Vendor configuration OR updated the Holiday schedule, then the vendor(s) would show on PQOH or Production orders
see screenshot below:

At this time, I cannot say specifically what or when a change occurred affecting this but as it was also showing like this in the UAT it would seem sometime before 2/20 when the data was refreshed on the UAT.

With only CC Produce and Roma having "Sunday" selected on their vendor setup under Inventory>Configuration>Vendor > select vendor > click Site Delivery Setting, only those would show up (2 settings working together). Also if you meant adding

Unfortunately, Primero does not store or display those production start/end dates directly on the placed order once it’s been submitted. The Production Orders screen uses those dates only as search filters, not as saved order attributes.

At this time, the only way to confirm which orders fall within specific production dates is exactly what you described: adjusting the date range on the Production Orders screen until the order appears in the results.

I agree this isn’t ideal,

- Missing FNS Warehous, Hardies, Southern Ice Cream.

- Production Plan Example:

- There is another site that has the same production plan but it has all the missing Vendors in Production Orders.

--- turn 2 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-05-22T14:45:35Z ---
Hello Stacey,

After further investigation. We have found the root cause of the issue.

In order to fix this issue, you will need to go to Inventory > Configuration > Vendors

and fix the Site delivery Schedule for each of the vendors in question.

For FNS Warehouse, you will need to fix the routes under Inventory > Warehouse Config > Routes

If you need further assistance, please feel free to call us at 866-442-6030 and ask for Chris.

TICKET 321248  |  Argyle ISD- Question about production order
==========================================================================================

--- turn 0 [customer/description] Amy Godwin <amy.godwin@argyleisd.com>  2026-05-27T20:44:25Z ---
Amy called with questions about production orders.

--- turn 1 [agent/private_note] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-05-27T20:48:50Z ---
Question:
Customer states that more items should be populating for Scott Gibson Middle School

A number of items listed on menu plans, such as P600188, are included in these menus (the vendor is the same that is listed in the order) and don't populate on the Orders.

Should these items (example
P600188
 ) appear in the order? I'm not sure how the system auto populates items in Production orders.

--- turn 2 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-05-28T12:34:06Z ---
Good morning Amy,

Is Scott Gibson a new school in the district? I'm finding that products are not set up to be orderable for them.

I selected a single menu item of Taco, Bacon, Egg & Cheese (LR1879) - and in reviewing the linked stock items, they are not orderable.

The easiest way to fix this, would be to go to Inventory > Configuration > Site Order Guide Set Up

From there, you can select "Configured Site" (which appears to be Argyle Middle School)

Then in the "Destination Site" - select "Scott Gibson" - and then click the button labeled "Copy"

This will set up Scott Gibson to have the same access to items that Argyle Middle does, and then the orders will function as expected.
